Here is the evidence-mode analysis of the FastAPI project.

---

## What This Project Is

**VERIFIED** — FastAPI (`fastapi/__init__.py:1`, version `0.136.1`) is a Python web framework for building APIs with standard type hints. It is a layer on top of **Starlette** (`fastapi/applications.py:41` — `class FastAPI(Starlette)`) and **Pydantic** (dependency: `pyproject.toml:46` — `pydantic>=2.9.0`). It auto-generates OpenAPI schemas and provides interactive docs (Swagger UI, ReDoc) out of the box. Maintained by Sebastián Ramírez (tiangolo). Repo: ~19,335 lines of framework code, **581 test files**, **2,122+ test functions** (`tests/`).

**VERIFIED** — Core modules:
- `fastapi/applications.py` (4,691 line) — `FastAPI` app class
- `fastapi/routing.py` (4,956 lines) — `APIRoute`, `APIRouter`, all path decorators
- `fastapi/param_functions.py` (2,460 lines) — `Path`, `Query`, `Body`, `Header`, `Cookie`, `Form`, `File`, `Depends`, `Security`
- `fastapi/dependencies/utils.py` (1,057 lines) — DI resolution engine
- `fastapi/openapi/utils.py` (606 lines) — OpenAPI schema generation
- `fastapi/security/` — OAuth2, HTTP auth, API key, OpenID Connect
- `fastapi/_compat/` — Pydantic v2 compatibility shim (`v2.py`)

---

## Strong Points

| # | Claim | Status | Evidence |
|---|-------|--------|----------|
| 1 | **Very high performance** — on par with NodeJS/Go via Starlette + Pydantic | **VERIFIED** | `README.md:34`: "*Very high performance, on par with NodeJS and Go (thanks to Starlette and Pydantic).*" Architecture: FastAPI delegates all HTTP handling to Starlette (ASGI), which is among the fastest Python frameworks. |
| 2 | **Automatic OpenAPI + JSON Schema generation from Python type hints** | **VERIFIED** | `fastapi/openapi/utils.py:60-177` — `get_openapi()` builds full OpenAPI 3.1 specs from route params, Pydantic models, docstrings. `pyproject.toml:41-50` depends on `pydantic>=2.9.0`. `param_functions.py` maps every Python type hint → OpenAPI parameter. |
| 3 | **Built-in dependency injection system** | **VERIFIED** | `fastapi/dependencies/utils.py:1-1057` — full DI engine: `solve_dependencies()`, `get_dependant()`, `get_parameterless_sub_dependant()`. Supports sub-dependencies, caching, scopes, async generators, context managers. |
| 4 | **Exceptional test coverage** | **VERIFIED** | 581 test files with 2,122 test functions covering edge cases: validation, security, dependencies, WebSockets, middleware, SSE, streaming, file uploads, OpenAPI schema correctness. |
| 5 | **First-class async support** | **VERIFIED** | Depends on `starlette>=0.46.0` (pure ASGI). `BackgroundTasks`, `concurrency.py` with `asynccontextmanager`, `run_in_threadpool`. WebSocket support in `websockets.py`. |
| 6 | **Rich security package** | **VERIFIED** | `fastapi/security/` has 7 modules: `oauth2.py` (693 lines), `http.py` (417 lines), `api_key.py` (320 lines), `open_id_connect_url.py` (94 lines). |
| 7 | **Mature deprecation hygiene** | **VERIFIED** | `FastAPIDeprecationWarning` (`exceptions.py:252`). Decorated deprecated items: `on_event` → lifespan (`routing.py:4924-4949`), `UJSONResponse`/`ORJSONResponse` → built-in JSON (`responses.py:39-81`). |
| 8 | **Compatibility layer for Pydantic versions** | **VERIFIED** | `fastapi/_compat/v2.py` (493 lines) handles differences across Pydantic v2.x releases with TODOs marking when shims can be removed. |

---

## Weak Points

| # | Claim | Status | Evidence |
|---|-------|--------|----------|
| 1 | **Monolithic routing module** — single file grows monotonically | **VERIFIED** | `fastapi/routing.py` is **4,956 lines**. Contains `APIRoute`, `APIRouter`, and every path operation decorator (`get`, `post`, `put`, `delete`, `patch`, `options`, `head`, `trace`). This is the single largest file and a coupling hotspot. |
| 2 | **`applications.py` is also very large** (4,691 lines) — combines app class, all metadata config, and lifespan logic | **VERIFIED** | Same pattern as routing.py. `FastAPI.__init__()` alone spans hundreds of lines for parameter documentation (`applications.py:57-4691`). Would benefit from decomposition. |
| 3 | **Multiple on_event → lifespan migration TODOs remain** | **VERIFIED** | `routing.py:1296,4872,4888,4904`: `"# TODO: remove this once the lifespan (or alternative) interface is improved"`. This indicates an incomplete migration path. |
| 4 | **`_compat/v2.py` accumulating Pydantic version shims with pending cleanup TODOs** | **VERIFIED** | `v2.py:58,73,99,179,191`: multiple `"# TODO: remove when dropping support for Pydantic < v2.12.3"` and similar. These are technical debt — version-specific workarounds that must be monitored. |
| 5 | **`get_openapi_operation_parameters` mixes schema generation with presentation concerns** | **VERIFIED** | `openapi/utils.py:107-177` — `_get_openapi_operation_parameters()` converts field metadata (deprecated, examples, descriptions, convert_underscores) inline with OpenAPI structure building. No separation between a schema model and its serialization. |
| 6 | **Dependency on both `python-multipart` and `multipart` detection is fragile** | **VERIFIED** | `dependencies/utils.py:94-120`: custom `ensure_multipart_is_installed()` tries to distinguish the correct `python-multipart` from the wrong `multipart` package by probing `parse_options_header`. Runtime errors are raised with hardcoded strings. |
| 7 | **No formal architecture documentation in-repo** | **VERIFIED** | `CONTRIBUTING.md:1` is a single sentence: *"Please read the Development - Contributing guidelines in the documentation site."* No ARCHITECTURE.md, ADRs, or architecture docs in the repo. |
| 8 | **OpenAPI generation is tightly coupled to the routing/dependency model** | **VERIFIED** | `openapi/utils.py` imports directly from `fastapi.routing`, `fastapi.dependencies.utils`, `fastapi.params`, `fastapi._compat`. It is not a standalone module — cannot be used independently of FastAPI's internal models. |

---

## Historical Context

- **Current version**: 0.136.1 (`__init__.py:3`)
- **Python requirement**: >=3.10 (`pyproject.toml:12`)
- **Key dependencies**: starlette>=0.46.0, pydantic>=2.9.0
- **Build system**: PDM (`pyproject.toml:2-3`)
- **Project status**: `"Development Status :: 4 - Beta"` in classifiers (`pyproject.toml:28`)
- **License**: MIT
- **Optional dependencies** (`pyproject.toml:59-77`): `fastapi-cli`, `httpx`, `jinja2`, `python-multipart`, `email-validator`, `uvicorn`, `pydantic-settings`, `pydantic-extra-types`
- **Legacy artifacts**: `routes`, `on_event`, `UJSONResponse`, `ORJSONResponse` all deprecated; `generate_operation_id()` deprecated in favor of `generate_operation_id_for_path()`

**UNKNOWN** — Cannot assess: open issue count, real-world adoption numbers, or security advisory status from this repo snapshot alone (no remote access available).

---

## Actionability Checklist

| Priority | Action | Effort | Impact |
|----------|--------|--------|--------|
| 🔴 | **`routing.py`** — split into modules (e.g., `routing/route.py`, `routing/router.py`, `routing/decorators.py`) | High | Reduces coupling hotspot, improves maintainability |
| 🔴 | **`applications.py`** — extract config/metadata into separate module | High | Same as above |
| 🟡 | Remove `on_event` TODO stubs (`routing.py:1296,4872+)` | Low | Cleans dead code path |
| 🟡 | Remove Pydantic compat shims when min-version >= 2.12.3 (`_compat/v2.py` TODOs) | Low | Reduces technical debt |
| 🟡 | Write **ARCHITECTURE.md** with module dependency diagram | Low | Onboarding, new contributors |
| 🟢 | Decompose `_get_openapi_operation_parameters()` — separate field metadata conversion from OpenAPI dict construction | Medium | Testability, readability |
| 🟢 | Replace hardcoded multipart detection strings with formal dependency declaration | Low | Error message hygiene |
| 🟢 | Audit all `# TODO` comments (23+ found) and file issues for each | Low | Technical debt tracking |
